>Tue, 29 Jan 2019 15:31:47 +0530

>Author: amolnin (amolnin@gmail.com)

>Commiter: amolnin (amolnin@gmail.com)

Due to boundary condition - when no of records was exactly in multiple
of batch-size, instead of breaking out of the loop, we were querying
cassandra one more time. Which was returning null - if no records found,
same situation was not handled.
Now handling null return value as well as fixing the boundray condition.

### Changes - to collapse the condition.
>Mon, 3 Dec 2018 14:49:07 +0530

>Author: amolnin (amolnin@gmail.com)

>Commiter: amolnin (amolnin@gmail.com)

Earlier:
if( orgId && externalOrgId not blank){
   if(orgId && derived Org Id from external Id not same){
     then throw error
    }
    return;
 else{
    if(externalid not blank)
      then use orgId from externalId
    else
      then use org Id directly
  }

  Due to this - when orgId & externalId were exactly same, the org id
value was not getting set at all.

### fixes for the issue. Actually - because of way conditions were put, in case both values orgid & externalid were given -> it was not at all storing org id.
